		// - pages links (numbers at top and bottom)
 var tafsir_btn_clicked=false;
function set_tafsir_pages_links() 

{

	$('.Paging a').click(function(){

		stat.tafsir.page = $(this).attr('href').replace(/^.*#/, '');

		refresh_screen();

		return false;

	});

}



// - scroll to section

function scroll_to_section(section)

{

	$el = $('#sec_' + section).eq(0);

	

	if ($el.size() > 0) {

		var p = $el.position().top; // - $('#sura').height();

		///if (typeof console != 'undefined') console.log('section = ' + section + ' P = ' + p + ', X = ' + u2p(p, $('#tafsir').attr('max')));

		var $slider = $("div[rel='text']").find('.space').eq(0);

		$slider.slider('value', u2p(p, $('#text').attr('max')));

	}

}



// - show tafsir

function show_tafsir(html, section) {

	$('#sura').removeClass('loading');

	$("#sura #text").html(html);

	$('<div class="clear"></div>').appendTo("#sura #text");

	

	set_tafsir_pages_links();

	reset_slider('text', true);

	scroll_to_section(section);

	

	var f1 = function () { reset_slider('text', false); };

	setTimeout(f1, 1000);

	

	var f2 = function () { fix_slider_max('text') }

	setTimeout(f2, 1000);

	setTimeout(f2, 3000);

	setTimeout(f2, 5000);

	

	if (playlist == null) player_new_sura();

}



// - find aya location

function tafsir_aya_location(aya_no) {

	var key = 'tafsir-pages-' + REVISION + '-' + stat.sura;

	var pages_code = localStorage.getItem(key);

	

	if (pages_code == null) {

		$.ajax({

			async: false,

			type: "get",

			url: 'tafsir-pages-' + stat.sura + '.js',

			success: function(response) {

				localStorage.setItem(key, response);

				pages_code = response;

			}

		});

	}

	

	var z = new Array();

	eval(pages_code);
//	Added by Odai    
    //    if(aya_no != 1)
    //        stat.tafsir.page = z[aya_no][0];
    if(tafsir_btn_clicked){
        stat.tafsir.page = (aya_no != 1) ? z[aya_no][0] : 1;
        tafsir_btn_clicked=false;
    }
    //    End by Odai
    //    stat.tafsir.page = (aya_no != 1) ? z[aya_no][0] : 1;
    //    Deleted by Odai

	var section = (aya_no != 1) ? z[aya_no][1] : 0;

	

	return section;

}



// - load tafsir

function load_tafsir(aya_no) {
if(aya_no==1)
{
aya_no=0;
}
	// - display loading

	$('#sura-body').hide();

	$('#sura #text').html('').scrollTop(0);

	$('#sura').addClass('loading');

	

	// - get aya page and section

	var section = 0;

	if (aya_no) section = tafsir_aya_location(aya_no);

	

	// - get data from localstorage

	var id = status_to_hash('sp');

	var key1 = 'tafsir-' + REVISION + '-' + id;

	var tafsir = localStorage.getItem(key1);

	

	if (tafsir != null) { // - load data when they are not ready

		show_tafsir(tafsir, section);

	} else { // - get from php if they are not saved

		$.ajax({

			type: "get",

			url: 'tafsir-' + id + '.html',

			success: function(response) {

				localStorage.setItem(key1, response);

				show_tafsir(response, section);

			}

		});

	}

	

	// - show sura information

	var key2 = 'sura-' + REVISION + '-' + stat.sura;

	sura_json = localStorage.getItem(key2);

	

	if (sura_json != null) { // - load data when they are not ready

		display_sura_data();

	} else { // - get from php if they are not saved

		$.ajax({

			type: "get",

			url: 'sura' + stat.sura + '.js',

			success: function(response) {

				sura_json = response;

				localStorage.setItem(key2, sura_json);

				display_sura_data();

			}

	   });

	}

	

	// - prepare aya selector

	if (sura_data != null) if (sura_data.ayas_count != $('#ayas > ul > li').size()) prepare_aya_selector(sura_data.ayas_count, aya_no);

}



// - go to aya in tafsir mode

function tafsir_goto_aya(aya_no) {

	// - get current page

	var key1 = status_to_hash('sp');	

	

	// - get aya page and section

	var section = 0;

	if (aya_no) section = tafsir_aya_location(aya_no);

	

	// - get new page

	var key2 = status_to_hash('sp');

	

	///if (typeof console != 'undefined') console.log('TAFSIR ' + aya_no + ' ' + key1 + ' ' + key2 + ' ' + section);

	

	// - go to aya

	if (key1 != key2) { // new page

		load_tafsir(aya_no);

	} else { // - current page

		scroll_to_section(section)

	}

	

	// - selector

	$('#ayas li.active').removeClass('active');

	$('#ayas a[href="#' + aya_no + '"]').parent().addClass('active');

	$("#ayas span.value").text(aya_no);

}

	    demodiv.style.left = ((($(window).width()-demodiv.offsetWidth)/2) + $(document).scrollLeft())+'px';		
	}
